###  Merituuli₁

* _This rare proper noun overlaps more common *Merituuli* (sea wind)_
* UPOS:  PROPN
* in KOTUS dictionary under:  24
* Origins: finer joukahainen 
* Possible NER class:  FIRST
* Blacklisted:  PROPN-BLOCKING
* Semantic tags:  FEMALE
